# <span data-ttu-id="ad892-104">Informations de version JavaScript</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ad892-104">JavaScript Version Information</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="ad892-105">La prise en charge de JavaScript varie en fonction des applications Microsoft Edge, Microsoft Store et de différents modes de document d’Internet Explorer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ad892-105">JavaScript support varies across Microsoft Edge, Microsoft Store apps, and different document modes of Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ad892-106">Pour plus d’informations sur le contrôle de version du code de document IE, voir définition de la [*compatibilité du document*](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=208537).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ad892-106">For more information about IE document code versioning, see [*Defining Document Compatibility*](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=208537).</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="ad892-107">Le tableau suivant résume la prise en charge JavaScript entre les applications Internet Explorer, Microsoft Edge et Microsoft Store.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ad892-107">The following table summarizes the JavaScript support across Internet Explorer, Microsoft Edge, and Microsoft Store apps.</span></span>  
  
> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="ad892-108">Fonctionnalités expérimentales \ (activé à *propos de: indicateurs*\) est indiqué par «exp».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ad892-108">Experimental features \(enabled from *about:flags*\) are indicated by "Exp."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ad892-109">Dans certains cas, la prise en charge des applications du Windows *Store* varie en fonction des applications Windows 8 \ (V8 \) et Windows 10 \ (version 10 \) et de la version de bureau de Windows, comme indiqué.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ad892-109">In some cases, *Store apps* support varies between Windows 8 \(v8\) and Windows 10 \(v10\) apps, and Windows desktop \(Win\) and Windows Phone \(Phone\), as indicated.</span></span>
